$(function(){initset()});
function initset(){
    $("#lest").mouseover(function(){$("#lest .in-box").show();}).mouseleave(function(){$("#lest .in-box").hide();});
    $(".mywanjiu").mouseover(function(){$(".mywanjiu .in-box").show();}).mouseleave(function(){$(".mywanjiu .in-box").hide();});
  	$("#member").mouseover(function(){$("#member .in-box").show();}).mouseleave(function(){$("#member .in-box").hide();});
  	$("#other").mouseover(function(){$("#other .in-box").show();}).mouseleave(function(){$("#other .in-box").hide();});
}
refreshCartNumCookie();
autoRefrshloginHeader();
function autoRefrshloginHeader(){
    // $(".loginMes").remove();
    if(Js.login.getAuth()){
        var userName = getCookie("COOKIE_NICKNAME");
        if(getCookie("COOKIE_LOGIN_TYPE")==2) userName = getCookie("CB_ShowMsg").replace(/%20/g," ");
        $("#loginMess").html('您好，尊敬的<a id="glUserName" href="'+_hrefPath+'/user/center/index.html">'+userName +'</a><a href="javascript:void(0)" onclick="Js.login.logout();return false;"> [退出]</a>');
    }else {
        $("#wjLogin").click(function () {
            Js.login.hasLogin(function () {
                location.reload();
            })
        })
    }
}
function headerLogin(){
    Js.login.hasLogin(typeof afterLoginCallback!="undefined"?afterLoginCallback:function(){autoRefrshloginHeader();addCookie("needReflesh", 1, 30*24*60*60);window.location.reload();});
}
function toRegister(){
	window.location.href="http://sso.letv.com/user/emailreg?next_action=http://www.wangjiu.com/wjproxy.html?jumpurl="+location.href;
}
function myWjcontent(){
    if(Js.login.getAuth())
        $("#myWjUserName").html('<a href="/user/center/index.html" target="_blank">'+$("#glUserName").text()+'</a>');
    else
        $("#myWjUserName").html('请<a href="javascript:void(0)" id="wjLogin">登录</a>');
    var products = getCookie("historyList")||"";
    var historyPid = products.split('.').reverse().join(',');
    $("#myWjContent").slideDown("fast");
    if(historyPid.length){
        Js.sendData(sendLink.prod+"api/web/query/getProductInfo.jsonp","pids="+historyPid,function(data){
            var products="";
            for(var i=0;i<data.result.length && i<5;i++){
                var item = data.result[i];
                products+='<div class="ct">'+
                  '<a href="'+_basePath+'product/product-pid-'+item.pid+'.html" target="_blank"><img title="'+item.productName+'" src="'+Js.getImagePath()+item.imageSrc+'_M5" /></a>'+
                  '<span><a href="'+_basePath+'product/product-pid-'+item.pid+'.html" target="_blank" title="'+item.productName+'">'+item.productName.substring(0,3)+'...</a></span>'+
                  '</div>';
            }
            $("#myWjProHistroyList").html(products);
            $("#myWjProHistroy").show();
        });
    }
}
function goUserCenter(){
   Js.login.hasLogin(function(){
      window.location.href=_hrefPath+"/user/center/index.html";
   });
}

}

   });
}
function AddFavorite(sURL, sTitle){
    try{window.external.addFavorite(sURL, sTitle);}catch (e){try{window.sidebar.addPanel(sTitle, sURL, "");}catch (e){alert("加入收藏失败，请使用Ctrl+D进行添加");}}
}

<script language="JavaScript">
window.pageConfig={next_action:"0"};
$(function(){
  $("#topMiniCart").mouseenter(function(){$(this).showMiniCart();});
    initSearch();
});
var sdcMenuList = $(".menu_cn").get();
var listEnter = false;
$(".menu_left").menuAim({
    rowSelector:".list",
    activate: function(row){
    //alert("dd "+$(row).prevAll().length);
      // var index = parseInt($(row).prevAll().length/2);
      var index = parseInt($(row).attr("data-index"));
      menuShow($(row),$(sdcMenuList[index]));
    },
    deactivate: function(row){
        // var index = parseInt($(row).prevAll().length/2);
        var index = parseInt($(row).attr("data-index"));
        $(sdcMenuList[index]).hide();
    },
    exit:function(row){
        listEnter=false;
        //  var index = parseInt($(row).prevAll().length/2);
      var index = parseInt($(row).attr("data-index"));
      //$(row).removeClass("mer");
        Js.Tools.pointerInElement(sdcMenuList[index],{callback:function(flag){
            if(flag==false && !listEnter){
              $(sdcMenuList[index]).hide();
              $(row).removeClass("mer");
            }
        }});
  },
  enter:function(row){
        $(".list").removeClass("mer");
        listEnter=true;
        if($(sdcMenuList[index]).is(":visible"))
        return;
        // var index = parseInt($(row).prevAll().length/2);
      var index = parseInt($(row).attr("data-index"));
      menuShow($(row),$(sdcMenuList[index]));
        $(row).addClass("mer");
  }
});
function menuShow(list,menu){
    if(!menu.length)
      return;
    var menuHeight = menu.outerHeight();
    var listCenter = list.position().top+list.height()/2;
    var top = listCenter-menuHeight/2;
    var windowTop = $(window).scrollTop();
    if(top<=0)
      top=35;
    var getTop = ($("#menuNav").offset().top-windowTop);
    menu.css("top",top<-getTop?-getTop:top);
    $(".menu_cn").hide();
    menu.show();
    var menuHY = menuHeight+(menu.offset().top-windowTop);
    if(menuHY>$(window).height()){
      var newTop = ($(window).height()-menuHeight - ($("#menuNav").offset().top-windowTop));
      menu.css("top",newTop<0?0:newTop);
    }
}
if(location.pathname!="/index.html"&&location.pathname!="/"){
    var width  = $("#shoppingMall").outerWidth();
    var height = $("#shoppingMall").outerHeight();
    $("#shoppingMall").mouseover(function(){
        // $(".menuNav").stop();
        // $(".menuNav").slideDown("fast");
        $("#menuNav").show();
        $("#menuNav").unbind("mouseleave").mouseleave(function(){
            $("#menuNav").hide();
        });
  }).unbind("mouseleave").mouseleave(function(e){
        if(($(this).offset().top-$(window).scrollTop()) - e.clientY<-30 )
            return;
      else
            $("#menuNav").hide();
  });
}
  function close(){
    //  alert(this);
    $("#hbfc").hide();
  }  
</script>

    //右侧购物车列表选中、未选中
    
  //右侧购物车
  $(function(){
     $(window).resize(function() {
         $(".box-cn").height($(window).height()-115);
     });
    /* $(window).on("scroll",function(){
　　　　$(".cart-box").hide();
　　 });*/
     $(".cart").click(function(){
        if($("#cart-box").is(":hidden")){
           $("#cart-box").show(500);
           $(".cartRightLoading").show();
            cartJsLib.listCart(0,0,function(data){
                if(data.result.length!=0){
                   $(".cartRightLoading").hide(500);
                   template.helper("parseInt",parseInt);
                   template.helper("parseFloat",parseFloat);
                   $("#cartRight").show();
                   $("#cartRight").html(Js.Tools.template("cartRightTemp", data));
                   $(".box-cn").height($(window).height()-115);
                   var checkboxSum=$(".checkTop").length;
                   var checkboxChecked=$(".checkTop:checked").length;
                   refreshCartNum(data);
                   //如果选中的个数等于总个数
                    if(checkboxSum==checkboxChecked){
                      $(".checkTopAll").attr("checked",true);
                    }else{
                      $(".checkTopAll").attr("checked",false);
                    }
                    //
                    $(".checkTop").bind("click",function(){
                        var checkboxSum=$(".checkTop").length;
                        console.info(123);
                        var checkboxChecked=$(".checkTop:checked").length;
                        if($(this).attr("checked")=="checked"){
                          cartJsLib.selectCart($(this).val(),0,1,1,function(data){
                              if(data.result!=""){
                                     refreshCartNum1(data);
                                     Iszengping(data);
                                }else{}
                            });
                        }else{
                             cartJsLib.selectCart($(this).val(),0,0,1,function(data){
                              if(data.result!=""){             
                                     refreshCartNum1(data);
                                     Iszengping(data);
                                }else{}
                             });
                        }
                        //如果选中的个数等于总个数
                        if(checkboxSum==checkboxChecked){
                          $(".checkTopAll").attr("checked",true);
                        }else{
                             $(".checkTopAll").attr("checked",false);
                        }   
                    });
                    //
                  
                    //清空购物车
                    $(".cleanEmptyCart").click(function(){
                         cartJsLib.cleanCart(0,function(data){
                            addCookie("cartNum",0);
                            $(".cartRight").hide(500);
                            $(".cartRightEmpty").show(500);
                            $(".topCartPrice").text(0);
                            $(".topCartNum").text(0);
                        });
                    });
                }else{
                    $(".box-cn").height($(window).height()-115);
                    $(".cartRightEmpty").show(500);
                     addCookie("cartNum",0);
                     $(".topCartPrice").text(0);
                     $(".topCartNum").text(0);
                  
                }
            });
          
        }else{
          $(".cart-box").hide();
        }
     });
    //二维码
    $(".bar-icon-ss").mouseover(function(){
      	$(".back-pop-2").show().css("z-index","1");
    }).mouseleave(function(){
        $(".back-pop-2").hide();
    });
    //我的收藏
    $(".bar-icon-sc").mouseover(function(){
      	$("#shoucang").show().css("z-index","1");;
    }).mouseleave(function(){
        $("#shoucang").hide();
    });
    //客服
    $(".bar-icon-pl").mouseover(function(){
        $("#kefu").show().css("z-index","1");;
    }).mouseleave(function(){
        $("#kefu").hide();
    });
    
  });
  //右侧购物车删除
  function deleteCartRight(this1,cartType,cartItemIds,needCartDetail){
          cartJsLib.deleteCart(cartType,cartItemIds,needCartDetail,function(data){
               if(data.result!=""){
                   $(this1).parents(".product").hide();
                   refreshCartNum(data); 
                   Iszengping(data);
                }else{
                   //console.info("购物车无商品了");
                   $(".box-cn").height($(window).height()-115);
                   refreshCartNum(data); 
                   $(".cartRight").hide();
                   $(".cartRightEmpty").show();
                }
          });
        
         
  }
  //右侧购物车数量加减
  function mit_maxRight(this1,max,min,cartType,cartItemIds,pids,purQuantity,needCartDetail){
        var u_p_num= $(this1).parent(".r").children(":input").val();
    
        if($(this1).hasClass("less")){
           u_p_num=--u_p_num;
          if(u_p_num<1){
             u_p_num=1
          }
        }else{
          if(u_p_num<max){
             u_p_num=++u_p_num;
          }
          
        }
        $(this1).parent(".r").children(":input").val(u_p_num);
        cartJsLib.updateCart(cartType,cartItemIds,pids,u_p_num,needCartDetail,function(data){
                   //单品最大购买数    最小购买数
                  if(data.result!=""){
                     $(".topCartPrice").html(data.result[0].sumPrice);
                      refreshCartNum(data);
                      
                  }else{
                    
                  }
          
          
        
        });
    
  }

//购物车通用库begin
var cartJsLib={
  listCart:function(cartType,TO_PAY,callback){
      var cartType=cartType||0 ;
        var TO_PAY=TO_PAY||0 ;
        var paramsList = "cartType="+cartType+"&TO_PAY="+TO_PAY;
        Js.sendData(sendLink.cart+"api/web/query/viewCart.jsonp",{param:paramsList},function(data){
          if(data.status == "1"){
                if(data.result[0] != undefined){
                  callback(data);
                }
                else{
                  callback(data);
                }
             }else{
               // alert("读取购物车失败,请联系客服");
             }
         }); 
    },
    addCart:function(p_id,pr_id,p_num,dt_id,prom_tag,callback){
        var p_id=p_id||0 ;
        var pr_id=pr_id||0 ;
        var p_num=p_num||1 ;
        var dt_id=dt_id||0;
        var prom_tag=prom_tag||1;
        var paramsAdd ="p_id="+p_id+"&pr_id="+pr_id+"&p_num="+p_num+"&dt_id="+dt_id+"&prom_tag="+prom_tag;
        Js.sendData(sendLink.cart+"api/web/insert/addCartItem.jsonp",{param:paramsAdd},function(data){
          if(data.status == "1"){
              callback(data);
              refreshCartNumLife(data);
              //alert("添加商品成功");
            }else{
              //console.info("添加商品失败");
            }
        });  
    },
    deleteCart:function(cartType,cartItemIds,needCartDetail,callback){
        var cartType=cartType||0 ;
        var paramsDelete = "cartType="+cartType+"&cartItemIds="+cartItemIds+"&needCartDetail="+needCartDetail;
        Js.sendData(sendLink.cart+"api/web/delete/delCartItem.jsonp",{param:paramsDelete},function(data){
            if(data.status == "1"){
              callback(data);
            }
        });
    },
    updateCart:function(cartType,cartItemIds,pids,purQuantity,needCartDetail,callback){
      var paramsUpdate = "cartType="+cartType+"&cartItemIds="+cartItemIds +"&pids="+pids+"&purQuantity="+purQuantity+"&needCartDetail="+needCartDetail;
      Js.sendData(sendLink.cart+"api/web/update/updCartItem.jsonp",{param:paramsUpdate},function(data){
            if(data.status == "1"){
                //console.info("更新商品成功");
                callback(data);
            }else{
                //console.info("更新商品失败");
            }
      });
    },
    selectCart:function(CART_ITEM_ID,PROMOTION_ID,STATUS,NEED_CART_DETAIL,callback){
      var paramsSelect = "CART_ITEM_ID="+CART_ITEM_ID+"&PROMOTION_ID="+PROMOTION_ID+"&STATUS="+STATUS+"&NEED_CART_DETAIL="+NEED_CART_DETAIL;
      Js.sendData(sendLink.cart+"api/web/update/uptCartItemStatus.jsonp",{param:paramsSelect},function(data){
            if(data.status == "1"){
                // console.info("选中和取消选中购物车的商品方法成功");
                callback(data);
            }else{
                //console.info("选中和取消选中购物车的商品方法失败");
            }
      });
    },
    cleanCart:function(uid,callback){
      var paramsSelect = "uid="+uid;
      Js.sendData(sendLink.cart+"api/web/delete/clearCart.jsonp",{param:paramsSelect},function(data){
            if(data.status == "1"){
                callback(data);
                //console.info("清空购物车成功");
            }else{
                //console.info("清空购物车失败");
            }
      });
    }
}
  //购物车通用库end
  //页头购物车删除
  function deleteCartTop(this1,cartType,cartItemIds,needCartDetail){
    cartJsLib.deleteCart(cartType,cartItemIds,needCartDetail,function(data){
        if(data.result.length!=0){
            $(this1).parents(".product").hide();
              refreshCartNum(data);
              Iszengping(data);
              //console.info("购物车内有商品");
          }else{
              //console.info("购物车无商品了");
              $("#cartListTop").hide();
              $(".cartTopEmpty").show();
              refreshCartNum(data);                  
          }
    });         
  }
  //判断购物车是否存在赠品信息
  function Iszengping (data){
        //增加多商家循环
      for(var j=0;j<data.result.length; j++){
         if(data.result[j].ORDER_PROMOTION && data.result[j].ORDER_PROMOTION.GIFT.length > 0){
           //有赠品信息
           $(".zengping").show(); 
           refreshCartNum(data);
         }else{
           //无赠品信息
           $(".zengping").hide();
           refreshCartNum(data);
         } 
      }
  }
  //价格工具类（js模板引擎而写）
  template.helper("newFixed",function(x){
      return toNewFixed(x);
  });
  function toNewFixed(x){
      var f_x = parseFloat(x);
      var f_x = Math.round(x * 100) / 100;
      var s_x = f_x.toString();
      var pos_decimal = s_x.indexOf('.');
      if (pos_decimal < 0) {
        pos_decimal = s_x.length;
        s_x += '.';
      }
      while (s_x.length <= pos_decimal + 2) {
        s_x += '0';
      }
      return s_x;
  }
  //返回顶部
  function pageScroll(){
      window.scrollBy(0,-1000);
      scrolldelay = setTimeout('pageScroll()',1);
      var sTop=document.documentElement.scrollTop+document.body.scrollTop;
      if(sTop==0) clearTimeout(scrolldelay);
  }
  function refreshCartNum(data){
  if(data.result.length!=0){
      var sump  = 0;
      var itemC = 0;
      for(var j=0;j<data.result.length; j++){
          sump  =sump.add(data.result[j].sumPrice);
          itemC +=parseInt(data.result[j].itemCount);
      }
      addCookie("cartNum",itemC,30*24*60*60);
      $(".topCartPrice").text(sump);
      $(".topCartNum").text(itemC);
    }else{
      addCookie("cartNum",0);
      $(".topCartPrice").text(0);
      $(".topCartNum").text(0);
    }
    refreshCartNumCookie();
}
function refreshCartNum1(data){
  if(data.result.length!=0){
        var sump  = 0;
      for(var j=0;j<data.result.length; j++){
          sump  += parseInt(data.result[j].sumPrice);
      }
      $(".topCartPrice").text(sump);
    }else{
      addCookie("cartNum",0);
      $(".topCartPrice").text(0);
      $(".topCartNum").text(0);
   }
   refreshCartNumCookie();
}
</script>

}

var sina = {
    $: function(objName) {
        if (document.getElementById) {
            return eval('document.getElementById("' + objName + '")')
        } else {
            return eval('document.all.' + objName)
        }
    },
    isIE: navigator.appVersion.indexOf("MSIE") != -1 ? true: false,
    addEvent: function(l, i, I) {
        if (l.attachEvent) {
            l.attachEvent("on" + i, I)
        } else {
            l.addEventListener(i, I, false)
        }
    },
    delEvent: function(l, i, I) {
        if (l.detachEvent) {
            l.detachEvent("on" + i, I)
        } else {
            l.removeEventListener(i, I, false)
        }
    },
    readCookie: function(O) {
        var o = "",
        l = O + "=";
        if (document.cookie.length > 0) {
            var i = document.cookie.indexOf(l);
            if (i != -1) {
                i += l.length;
                var I = document.cookie.indexOf(";", i);
                if (I == -1) I = document.cookie.length;
                o = unescape(document.cookie.substring(i, I))
            }
        };
        return o
    },
    writeCookie: function(i, l, o, c) {
        var O = "",
        I = "";
        if (o != null) {
            O = new Date((new Date).getTime() + o * 3600000);
            O = "; expires=" + O.toGMTString()
        };
        if (c != null) {
            I = ";domain=" + c
        };
        document.cookie = i + "=" + escape(l) + O + I
    },
    readStyle: function(I, l) {
        if (I.style[l]) {
            return I.style[l]
        } else if (I.currentStyle) {
            return I.currentStyle[l]
        } else if (document.defaultView && document.defaultView.getComputedStyle) {
            var i = document.defaultView.getComputedStyle(I, null);
            return i.getPropertyValue(l)
        } else {
            return null
        }
    }
};

//滚动图片构造函数
//UI&UE Dept. mengjia
//080623
function ScrollPic(scrollContId, arrLeftId, arrRightId, dotListId) {
    this.scrollContId = scrollContId;
    this.arrLeftId = arrLeftId;
    this.arrRightId = arrRightId;
    this.dotListId = dotListId;
    this.dotClassName = "dotItem";
    this.dotOnClassName = "dotItemOn";
    this.dotObjArr = [];
    this.pageWidth = 0;
    this.frameWidth = 0;
    this.speed = 10;
    this.space = 10;
    this.pageIndex = 0;
    this.autoPlay = true;
    this.autoPlayTime = 5;
    var _autoTimeObj, _scrollTimeObj, _state = "ready";
    this.stripDiv = document.createElement("DIV");
    this.listDiv01 = document.createElement("DIV");
    this.listDiv02 = document.createElement("DIV");
    if (!ScrollPic.childs) {
        ScrollPic.childs = []
    };
    this.ID = ScrollPic.childs.length;
    ScrollPic.childs.push(this);
    this.initialize = function() {
        if (!this.scrollContId) {
            throw new Error("必须指定scrollContId.");
            return
        };
        this.scrollContDiv = sina.$(this.scrollContId);
        if (!this.scrollContDiv) {
            throw new Error("scrollContId不是正确的对象.(scrollContId = \"" + this.scrollContId + "\")");
            return
        };
        this.scrollContDiv.style.width = this.frameWidth + "px";
        this.scrollContDiv.style.overflow = "hidden";
        this.listDiv01.innerHTML = this.listDiv02.innerHTML = this.scrollContDiv.innerHTML;
        this.scrollContDiv.innerHTML = "";
        this.scrollContDiv.appendChild(this.stripDiv);
        this.stripDiv.appendChild(this.listDiv01);
        this.stripDiv.appendChild(this.listDiv02);
        this.stripDiv.style.overflow = "hidden";
        this.stripDiv.style.zoom = "1";
        this.stripDiv.style.width = "32766px";
       if(!+[1,]){this.listDiv01.style.styleFloat="left";this.listDiv02.style.styleFloat="left";}else
       {this.listDiv01.style.cssFloat="left";this.listDiv02.style.cssFloat="left";}
        sina.addEvent(this.scrollContDiv, "mouseover", Function("ScrollPic.childs[" + this.ID + "].stop()"));
        sina.addEvent(this.scrollContDiv, "mouseout", Function("ScrollPic.childs[" + this.ID + "].play()"));
        if (this.arrLeftId) {
            this.arrLeftObj = sina.$(this.arrLeftId);
            if (this.arrLeftObj) {
                sina.addEvent(this.arrLeftObj, "mousedown", Function("ScrollPic.childs[" + this.ID + "].rightMouseDown()"));
                sina.addEvent(this.arrLeftObj, "mouseup", Function("ScrollPic.childs[" + this.ID + "].rightEnd()"));
                sina.addEvent(this.arrLeftObj, "mouseout", Function("ScrollPic.childs[" + this.ID + "].rightEnd()"))
            }
        };
        if (this.arrRightId) {
            this.arrRightObj = sina.$(this.arrRightId);
            if (this.arrRightObj) {
                sina.addEvent(this.arrRightObj, "mousedown", Function("ScrollPic.childs[" + this.ID + "].leftMouseDown()"));
                sina.addEvent(this.arrRightObj, "mouseup", Function("ScrollPic.childs[" + this.ID + "].leftEnd()"));
                sina.addEvent(this.arrRightObj, "mouseout", Function("ScrollPic.childs[" + this.ID + "].leftEnd()"))
            }
        };
        if (this.dotListId) {
            this.dotListObj = sina.$(this.dotListId);
            if (this.dotListObj) {
                var pages = Math.round(this.listDiv01.offsetWidth / this.frameWidth + 0.4),
                i,
                tempObj;
                for (i = 0; i < pages; i++) {
                    tempObj = document.createElement("span");
                    this.dotListObj.appendChild(tempObj);
                    this.dotObjArr.push(tempObj);
                    if (i == this.pageIndex) {
                        tempObj.className = this.dotClassName
                    } else {
                        tempObj.className = this.dotOnClassName
                    };
                    tempObj.title = "第" + (i + 1) + "页";
                    sina.addEvent(tempObj, "click", Function("ScrollPic.childs[" + this.ID + "].pageTo(" + i + ")"))
                }
            }
        };
        if (this.autoPlay) {
            this.play()
        }
    };
    this.leftMouseDown = function() {
        if (_state != "ready") {
            return
        };
        _state = "floating";
        _scrollTimeObj = setInterval("ScrollPic.childs[" + this.ID + "].moveLeft()", this.speed)
    };
    this.rightMouseDown = function() {
        if (_state != "ready") {
            return
        };
        _state = "floating";
        _scrollTimeObj = setInterval("ScrollPic.childs[" + this.ID + "].moveRight()", this.speed)
    };
    this.moveLeft = function() {
        if (this.scrollContDiv.scrollLeft + this.space >= this.listDiv01.scrollWidth) {
            this.scrollContDiv.scrollLeft = this.scrollContDiv.scrollLeft + this.space - this.listDiv01.scrollWidth
        } else {
            this.scrollContDiv.scrollLeft += this.space
        };
        this.accountPageIndex()
    };
    this.moveRight = function() {
        if (this.scrollContDiv.scrollLeft - this.space <= 0) {
            this.scrollContDiv.scrollLeft = this.listDiv01.scrollWidth + this.scrollContDiv.scrollLeft - this.space
        } else {
             this.scrollContDiv.scrollLeft -= this.space
        };
        this.accountPageIndex()
    };
    this.leftEnd = function() {
        if (_state != "floating") {
            return
        };
        _state = "stoping";
        clearInterval(_scrollTimeObj);
        var fill = this.pageWidth - this.scrollContDiv.scrollLeft % this.pageWidth;
        this.move(fill)
    };
    this.rightEnd = function() {
        if (_state != "floating") {
            return
        };
        _state = "stoping";
        clearInterval(_scrollTimeObj);
        var fill = -this.scrollContDiv.scrollLeft % this.pageWidth;
        this.move(fill)
    };
    this.move = function(num, quick) {
        var thisMove = num / 5;
        if (!quick) {
            if (thisMove > this.space) {
                thisMove = this.space
            };
            if (thisMove < -this.space) {
                thisMove = -this.space
            }
        };
        if (Math.abs(thisMove) < 1 && thisMove != 0) {
            thisMove = thisMove >= 0 ? 1 : -1
        } else {
            thisMove = Math.round(thisMove)
        };
        var temp = this.scrollContDiv.scrollLeft + thisMove;
        if (thisMove > 0) {
            if (this.scrollContDiv.scrollLeft + thisMove >= this.listDiv01.scrollWidth) {
                this.scrollContDiv.scrollLeft = this.scrollContDiv.scrollLeft + thisMove - this.listDiv01.scrollWidth
            } else {
                this.scrollContDiv.scrollLeft += thisMove
            }
        } else {
            if (this.scrollContDiv.scrollLeft - thisMove <= 0) {
                this.scrollContDiv.scrollLeft = this.listDiv01.scrollWidth + this.scrollContDiv.scrollLeft - thisMove
            } else {
                this.scrollContDiv.scrollLeft += thisMove
            }
        };
        num -= thisMove;
        if (Math.abs(num) == 0) {
            _state = "ready";
            if (this.autoPlay) {
                this.play()
            };
            this.accountPageIndex();
            return
        } else {
            this.accountPageIndex();
            setTimeout("ScrollPic.childs[" + this.ID + "].move(" + num + "," + quick + ")", this.speed)
        }
    };
    this.next = function() {
        if (_state != "ready") {
            return
        };
        _state = "stoping";
        this.move(this.pageWidth, true)
    };
    this.play = function() {
        if (!this.autoPlay) {
            return
        };
        clearInterval(_autoTimeObj);
        _autoTimeObj = setInterval("ScrollPic.childs[" + this.ID + "].next()", this.autoPlayTime * 1000)
    };
    this.stop = function() {
        clearInterval(_autoTimeObj)
    };
    this.pageTo = function(num) {
        if (_state != "ready") {
            return
        };
        _state = "stoping";
        var fill = num * this.frameWidth - this.scrollContDiv.scrollLeft;
        this.move(fill, true)
    };
    this.accountPageIndex = function() {
        this.pageIndex = Math.round(this.scrollContDiv.scrollLeft / this.frameWidth);
        if (this.pageIndex > Math.round(this.listDiv01.offsetWidth / this.frameWidth + 0.4) - 1) {
            this.pageIndex = 0
        };
        var i;
        for (i = 0; i < this.dotObjArr.length; i++) {
            if (i == this.pageIndex) {
                this.dotObjArr[i].className = this.dotClassName
            } else {
                this.dotObjArr[i].className = this.dotOnClassName
            }
        }
    }
};
	  		</script>
<script type="text/text" id="flashPromotionListTemp"><%var index=0;%><%for(var i=0;i<result.length;i++){%><%if(index<7){%><%var p=result[i];var secToBegin=formatTime(p.secToBegin).split(":");var secToEnd=formatTime(p.secToEnd).split(":");var timeInfo='00时00分00秒';var day=parseInt(secToEnd[0])>0?secToEnd[0]+"天":"";if(p.remainingQuantity>0&&p.secToEnd>0)timeInfo=day+secToEnd[1]+'时'+secToEnd[2]+'分'+secToEnd[3]+"秒";%><%if(p.remainingQuantity>0&&p.secToEnd>0){%><%index=index+1;var imgPath=getImagePath(p.source)%><dd startSeconds="<%=p.secToBegin%>" endSeconds="<%=p.secToEnd%>" style="<%if(index==6){%>border-right:0;<%}%>"><div class="list-box"><div class="time"><font class="f_red"><%=timeInfo%></font></div><div class="p-img"><a href="/product/product-pid-<%=p.productId%>.html" target="_blank" class="cartFly"><img alt="<%=p.productName%>" src="<%=imgPath%>!105x420.gif" title="<%=p.productName%>"></a></div><div class="p-name"><a class="a-text01" target="_blank" href="/product/product-pid-<%=p.productId%>.html" title="<%=p.productName%>"><%=p.productName%></a></div><div class="p-price">闪购价：<b><%=parseInt(p.finalPrice)%></b></div><div class="p-pce">￥<%=parseInt(p.price)%></div><a class="butn addToCart" ctags="0|3|1" levelId="<%=p.userLevelMin%>" num="<%=p.minLimitNum%>" pids="<%=p.productId%>">加入购物车</a></div></dd><%}%><%}%><%}%></script>

<script type='text/javascript'>
$(function(){
    getFlashPromotionList();
    specialEffects();
    // setTimeout(function(){ zpq_tuiguang("index"); },100); //晶赞
});
function specialEffects(){
    $(".tab-menu").find("li").unbind("mouseenter").bind("mouseenter", function(){
        $(this).addClass("on").siblings().removeClass();
        $(".sale > dl").hide().eq($('.tab-menu li').index(this)).show();
    });
    $(".ad-news-top").find("li").unbind("mouseenter").bind("mouseenter", function(){
        $(this).addClass("currt").siblings().removeClass();
        $(".ad-news > dl").hide().eq($('.ad-news-top li').index(this)).show();
    });
    $(".column01 li").unbind("mouseenter").bind("mouseenter", function(){
        $(".column01 li").hide();
        $(this).show();         
        $(this).find("div[class='column-list']").show();
        $(this).find("div[name='scan']").append("<div class='meng'></div>");
    });
    $(".column01").unbind("mouseleave").bind("mouseleave", function(){
        $(".column01 li").show();
        $(".column-list").hide();
        $(this).find("div[class='meng']").remove();
    });
}
function getFlashPromotionList(){
    flashType = 0;
    userLevel = "1,2";
    var params = "NO_RECOMMEND=1&userLevel="+userLevel+"&flashType="+flashType;
    Js.sendData(sendLink.prom+"api/web/query/getFlashPromotionList.jsonp",{async:true,param:params},function(data){
        if(data.status == 1 && typeof data.result != "undefined" && data.result.length > 0){
            template.helper("formatTime",formatTime);
            template.helper("parseInt",parseInt);
            template.helper("getImagePath",Js.getImageByName);
            $("#flashPromotion").html(Js.Tools.template("flashPromotionListTemp",data));
            promotionSetTime();
        }
    });
}
function promotionSetTime(){
    $(".sale").find("dd").each(function(){
        var _this      = $(this);
        var startTime  = _this.attr("startSeconds");
        var endSeconds = _this.attr("endSeconds");
        var elem       = _this.find("font");
        if(endSeconds != "" && endSeconds <= 0)
            getFlashPromotionList();
        else
            countDown(startTime, endSeconds, elem);
    });
}
function formatTime(second) {
    return [parseInt(second/60/60/24), parseInt(second/60/60%24), parseInt(second/60%60), second%60].join(":").replace(/\b(\d)\b/g, "0$1");
}
function countDown(beginTime, endTime, elem){
    var timer = setInterval(function(){
        if (endTime > 0) {
            endTime  -= 1;
            var day     = Math.floor((endTime / 3600) / 24);
            var hour    = Math.floor((endTime / 3600) % 24);
            var minute  = Math.floor((endTime / 60) % 60);
            var second  = Math.floor(endTime % 60);
            if(day < 0){day = 0;}
            if(hour < 0){hour = 0;}
            if(minute < 0){minute = 0;}
            if(second < 0){second = 0;}
            var daytemp = day<10?"0"+day:day;
            $(elem).text((day>0?daytemp+"天":"")+(hour<10?"0"+hour:hour)+"时"+(minute<10?"0"+minute:minute)+"分"+(second<10?"0"+second:second)+"秒");
        } else { 
            clearInterval(timer);
        }
    }, 1000);
}
</script>
